<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3"><a href = vnd.unilang:etymology.html>Etymology</a> 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<div class="sister-wikipedia sister-project noprint floatright" style="border: 1px solid aaa; font-size: 90%; background: f9f9f9; width: 250px; padding: 4px; text-align: left;"><div style="float: left;"><div class="floatnone"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/44px-Wikipedia-logo.png" decoding="async" width="44" height="44" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/66px-Wikipedia-logo.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/88px-Wikipedia-logo.png 2x" data-file-width="200" data-file-height="200" /></div></div><div style="margin-left: 60px;"><a href = vnd.unilang:english.html>English</a> Wikipedia <a href = vnd.unilang:have.html>has</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:an.html>an</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:article.html>article</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:on.html>on</a>:<div style="margin-left: 10px;"><b class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Spivak_pronouns" class="extiw" title="w:Spivak pronouns">Spivak pronouns</a></b></div></div><span class="interProject"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Spivak_pronouns" class="extiw" title="w:Spivak pronouns">Wikipedia </a></span></div>
<p>Coined <a href = vnd.unilang:by.html>by</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:christine.html>Christine</a> M. Elverson <a href = vnd.unilang:by.html>by</a> removing <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> "th" <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:them.html>them</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:perhaps.html>perhaps</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:influence.html>influenced</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:by.html>by</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> pre-existing <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:em.html>em</a></i>/<i class="Latn mention" lang="en">'<a href = vnd.unilang:em.html>em</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:now.html>now</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:often.html>often</a> perceived <a href = vnd.unilang:as.html>as</a> apheretic <a href = vnd.unilang:form.html>forms</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:them.html>them</a></i> (<a href = vnd.unilang:though.html>though</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:originally.html>originally</a> unrelated).
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun"><a href = vnd.unilang:pronoun.html>Pronoun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
